                        <div data-reactid="933">
                         This bright, spacious room is off an exterior corridor on the second floor, with a separate keyed entrance for your privacy. There is a double and a single bed, a desk and chair, a sitting area, and a full bathroom. Enjoy great mountain views.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="934">
                         Our home is nestled in the hills on the outskirts of Tlaxcala City (two miles from downtown Tlaxcala). Enjoy our large garden, patio, and second-floor terrace with panoramic views. We provide in-room bottled water, hair dryer, toiletries, and clock radio. There is WiFi throughout the property. We have a second-story private guest lounge with cable TV, DVD player, books, maps and tourist information, dining area, and a kitchenette with microwave, small refrigerator, hot plate, coffee maker and toaster. We have a washing machine and clotheslines on the third floor that guests are welcome to use. We will lend you a bike to explore the surrounding countryside if you like.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="935">
                         Tlaxcala is one of the very safest places in Mexico. There are few foreign tourists here, and the local people are very warm and welcoming. If you enjoy the outdoors, you can hike up into the surrounding hills or along the river, visit the National Park on the Malinche volcano, or bike ride through the surrounding countryside. Tlaxcala city offers many museums, a beautiful plaza, a wide variety of restaurants and coffee shops, the traditional open-air market on Saturdays, local handcrafts, and lovely colonial architecture. Our little town of San Juan Totolac has many traditional fairs and religious festivals throughout the year, as do neighboring villages, and you are welcome to participate in these expressions of local culture.
                        </div>
